          <h1 class="title" style="background: transparent; border-width: 0px">
           Enjoy - Food &amp; Travel

         </div>
         <div class="descriptionwrapper">
          <p class="description">
           <span>
            Enjoy Food &amp; Travel is a website for you that appreciate good food, wine and beer. Our team will share memorable food memories and recipes from Scandinavia and beyond. Enjoy Food &amp; Travel will provide information on how to get the best and cheapest transportation to your  destination, and how to get an affordable deal on accommodation. Enjoy Food &amp; Travel will also deal with the options you have to do research on the net on the city or region you plan to visit before you leave.
           </span>
          </p>

      <div id="main-wrapper">
       <div class="main section" id="main">
        <div class="widget Blog" data-version="1" id="Blog1">
         <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
          <div class="date-outer">
           <h2 class="date-header">
            <span>
             Wednesday, April 24, 2013
            </span>
           </h2>
           <div class="date-posts">
            <div class="post-outer">
             <div class="post hentry">
              <a name="8794039921482435898">
              </a>
              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/04/coming-june-july-2013-madrid-barcelona.html">
                COMING JUNE-JULY 2013: Madrid, Barcelona and Sitges - Spain
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <iframe frameborder="0" height="480" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" scrolling="no" src="https://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.00043d90df713d3c0e7af&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;ll=44.684277,3.999023&amp;spn=14.99614,28.125&amp;z=5&amp;iwloc=0004da9069a5f26d8ed37&amp;output=embed" width="640">
                </iframe>
                <br/>
                <small>
                 Vis
                 <a href="https://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.00043d90df713d3c0e7af&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;ll=44.684277,3.999023&amp;spn=14.99614,28.125&amp;z=5&amp;iwloc=0004da9069a5f26d8ed37&amp;source=embed" style="color: blue; text-align: left;">
                  Spain on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel 2006-2013
                 </a>
                 i et større kart
                </small>
                <br/>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <i>
                  These last Norwegian summers have been too cold and humid for most of us, and to ensure an adquate dose of sun and summer Enjoy Food &amp; Travel pack up and leave for lovely Spain two weeks in June and July 2013.
                 </i>
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8i-D1qALmvQ/UXdul8E45AI/AAAAAAAAQ6Y/TBfeaU9NOrc/s1600/hotel-gran-versalles-madrid-fachada-01.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="200" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8i-D1qALmvQ/UXdul8E45AI/AAAAAAAAQ6Y/TBfeaU9NOrc/s320/hotel-gran-versalles-madrid-fachada-01.jpg" width="320"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     Gran Versalles**** (Photo courtesy  Hotel website)
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 Our last trip to Spain was in 2011, when we stayed for a week in Sitges. We both agreed that that was too little, and this summer we decided that we would stay for at least two weeks.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 We discovered that air fare had skyrocketed when we started looking for tickets a few weeks ago. But we managed to get reasonably priced fare.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 We will fly to Madrid with Norwegian Air Shuttle, leaving Oslo Airport 7.40 AM, arriving Copenhagen 8.50 AM. At
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kastrup_Airport" target="_blank">
                  Kastrup Airport
                 </a>
                 we have a one hour and ten minutes to our flight to
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madrid_Barajas" target="_blank">
                  Madrid Barajas
                 </a>
                 where we arrive at 1.10 PM.
                 <br/>
                 <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: left; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lG3oNYnFLw8/UXdvwpY1x1I/AAAAAAAAQ6k/xL_7zWNFREU/s1600/Atenea_Calabria_lowres_20_1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="213" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-lG3oNYnFLw8/UXdvwpY1x1I/AAAAAAAAQ6k/xL_7zWNFREU/s320/Atenea_Calabria_lowres_20_1.jpg" width="320"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     Aparthotel Atenea Calabria *** (Photo:  Hotel website)
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 Price paid for two: NOK 3308,- (432 Euros / 565 USD), hardly a rip-off for air fare during high season.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 We will stay three nights at
                 <a href="http://www.hotelgranversalles.es/en/" target="_blank">
                  Gran Versalles
                 </a>
                 ****, close to the famous Prado Museum. Our 18 square metre / 193 square feet of the Spanish capital cost us around 304 NOK (40, 5 Euros / 52,80 USD) per person per night. Compared to Norway this is dead cheap. It does not include breakfast.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 After three nights, we plan to catch the
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Madrid%E2%80%93Barcelona_high-speed_rail_line" target="_blank">
                  high speed train service from Madrid to Barcelona
                 </a>
                 . The 621 km (386 mile) journey takes less than three hours.
                 <br/>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                 </div>
                 <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2007/06/barcelona-from-z-to-make-it-easier-for.html" target="_blank">
                  I've been to Barcelona several times before
                 </a>
                 , but this time we are excited to stay in a one room apartment with our own kitchen in
                 <a href="http://www.aparthotelateneacalabria.com/es/" target="_blank">
                  Aparthotel Athaenea Calabria
                 </a>
                 *** in the
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eixample" target="_blank">
                  Eixample
                 </a>
                 area. The 35 square meter (376 square feet) apartment  cost us 375,54 NOK (Euros 50 / 65 USD), including breakfast. I do look forward to do some home cooking in the Catalan capital.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">
                     <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-y3SwQjSY5xg/UXdwWTLwOUI/AAAAAAAAQ60/9jhfrKuupp4/s1600/Doble-Exterior.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                      <img border="0" height="156" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-y3SwQjSY5xg/UXdwWTLwOUI/AAAAAAAAQ60/9jhfrKuupp4/s400/Doble-Exterior.jpg" width="400"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                   <tr>
                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     Subur*** (Photo courtesy  Hotel website)
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 After another three nights we head for the beach.
                 <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2008/06/short-guide-to-sitges-view-larger-map.html" target="_blank">
                  The vibrant resort town of Sitges
                 </a>
                 is located a half hour train ride south of Barcelona, and this is a destination I look forward to return to.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 Last time, we stayed at Hotel Port Sitges Resort, outside the city centre. In spite of the comfort of a spacious two room apartments, we felt isolated from the vibrant night life in the area by the main beach. Now we have booked a double room with balcony at
                 <a href="http://www.hotelsubur.com/sitgeshotel/eng/index.html" target="_blank">
                  Subur***
                 </a>
                 , located at the beach. In spite of the location, even this hotel is no rip-off. We pay less than NOK 350 (46 Euros / 60 USD) per night. This does not include breakfast, but who cares. There are dozens of reasonably priced breakfast cafes nearby.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 8 nights by the beach to be looking forward to, before our return Vueling flight from Barcelona to Oslo. NOK 1957 for two in July is a bargain.
                 <br/>
                 <b>
                  <br/>
                 </b>
                 <b>
                  Final costs for trip
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 The final cost of air fare and accommodation for two weeks per person is:
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   Airfare Oslo-Copenhagen-Madrid (Norwegian Air Shuttle): NOK 1654,-, EUR 219,60 (Supersaver.no)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Accommodation Gran Versalles****, Madrid (3 nights): NOK 913,-,  EUR 121, 50 (Booking.com)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Accommodation Aparthotel Atenea Calabria*** , Barcelona (3 nights): NOK 1127,-,  EUR 150 (Booking.com)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Accommodation Subur, Sitges*** (8 nights): NOK 2794,-,  EUR 372,- (Booking.com)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Airfare Barcelona-Oslo (Vueling): NOK 953,50,  EUR 130 (Bravofly.no)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   TOTAL: NOK 7466,-, EUR 993,-
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div style="clear: both;">
               </div>
              </div>

           <h2 class="date-header">
            <span>
             Thursday, April 11, 2013
            </span>
           </h2>
           <div class="date-posts">
            <div class="post-outer">
             <div class="post hentry">
              <a name="8280183838884726748">
              </a>
              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/04/the-new-jewish-synagogue-berlin.html">
                The New Jewish Synagogue, Berlin
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-K8OCGJyvW84/UWbxvLBg9FI/AAAAAAAAQ6A/K7Kg81Yf7qI/s1600/IMGP9330.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="300" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-K8OCGJyvW84/UWbxvLBg9FI/AAAAAAAAQ6A/K7Kg81Yf7qI/s400/IMGP9330.JPG" width="400"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    The beautiful dome of the New Synagogue
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <i>
                  Close to Hackisher Markt in Berlin, you find the
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Synagogue_%28Berlin%29" target="_blank">
                   New Synagogue
                  </a>
                  - a remarkable building. What you see is just a fraction of what this structure used to hold.
                 </i>
                </div>
                <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-6IQ3B9JI10Q/UWb1LKbPRXI/AAAAAAAAQ6I/JbfNzv7-pVE/s1600/IMGP9332.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="240" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-6IQ3B9JI10Q/UWb1LKbPRXI/AAAAAAAAQ6I/JbfNzv7-pVE/s320/IMGP9332.JPG" width="320"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    The two side towers underline its Moorish influence
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 In Oranienburg Strasse in Berlin you find an awesome historic monument. The beautiful New Synagogue was built in 1866
                 <i>
                 </i>
                 and was
                 <i>
                 </i>
                 inaugurated by the famous
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Otto_von_Bismarck" target="_blank">
                  Count Otto von Bismarck
                 </a>
                 .
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 Sadly, the present building is a reconstruction after it was badly damaged by fire during the
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kristallnacht" target="_blank">
                  Kristallnacht
                 </a>
                 prior to World War II.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 It was a huge building when it was built, seating more than 3 000 people. What is left, however, is mainly the magnificent facade and a few rooms behind it.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 I would love to visit the huge golden dome, that is open to public, and maybe I will, as I will return to Berlin in a months time.
                </div>
                <iframe frameborder="0" height="480" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" scrolling="no" src="https://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.000440248c42299cdb83d&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;ll=52.526783,13.397119&amp;spn=0.006266,0.013733&amp;z=16&amp;iwloc=0004da197365b802b4354&amp;output=embed" width="640">
                </iframe>
                <br/>
                <small>
                 Vis
                 <a href="https://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.000440248c42299cdb83d&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;ll=52.526783,13.397119&amp;spn=0.006266,0.013733&amp;z=16&amp;iwloc=0004da197365b802b4354&amp;source=embed" style="color: blue; text-align: left;">
                  Berlin on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel
                 </a>
                 i et større kart
                </small>
               </div>
               <div style="clear: both;">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="post-footer">
               <script charset="utf-8" src="http://feeds.feedburner.com/~s/Enjoy-FoodTravel?i=http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/04/the-new-jewish-synagogue-berlin.html" type="text/javascript">

              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/food-stories-on-enjoy-food-travel-2013.html">
                Food stories on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel 2013
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                 <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-o6uV6SpykDY/UUFWdaImuPI/AAAAAAAAQ2w/4Jz9ocUgJo8/s1600/P1030127.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                  <img border="0" height="225" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-o6uV6SpykDY/UUFWdaImuPI/AAAAAAAAQ2w/4Jz9ocUgJo8/s400/P1030127.JPG" width="400"/>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <br/>
                <i>
                 Here is a list of food stories published on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel 2013
                </i>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <b>
                 E
                </b>
                <br/>
                <ul style="text-align: left;">
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/01/end-of-shelf-life-discounts.html">
                   End of shelf life discounts
                  </a>
                  <i>
                   <br/>
                  </i>
                  Look for discounts for products at the end of their shelf life. I did today and stocked up quality food for my freezer
                  <b>
                  </b>
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <b>
                 P
                </b>
                <br/>
                <ul style="text-align: left;">
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/paella-for-dinner.html">
                   Paella for dinner
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <i>
                   Paella, the Spanish Risotto originating from the Valencia Region is a inexpensive, simple and tasty dinner.
                  </i>
                 </li>
                </ul>

           <div class="date-posts">

              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/new-and-better-direct-flights-from_25.html">
                NEW AND BETTER: Direct flights from Bergen Airport
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <iframe frameborder="0" height="480" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" scrolling="no" src="https://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.0004708b613b68cad72b1&amp;hl=no&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;ll=65.658275,70.3125&amp;spn=80.823559,225&amp;z=2&amp;iwloc=0004708b6e235c84fec9a&amp;output=embed" width="640">
                </iframe>
                <br/>
                <small>
                 Vis
                 <a href="https://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.0004708b613b68cad72b1&amp;hl=no&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;ll=65.658275,70.3125&amp;spn=80.823559,225&amp;z=2&amp;iwloc=0004708b6e235c84fec9a&amp;source=embed" style="color: blue; text-align: left;">
                  MARCH 2013: All non-stop flights from Bergen Airport
                 </a>
                 i et større kart
                </small>
                <br/>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <i>
                  This new and improved map shows domestic, charter and international 
 direct flights operated by all airlines from Bergen Flesland Airport. It shows 
 seasonal as well as flights running all year.
                 </i>
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 It is based on information from the Bergen Flesland Airport official website. Errors 
 may occur. Do consult airport website or airline for updated 
 information.
                </div>
                <ul style="text-align: justify;">
                 <li style="text-align: justify;">
                  Red marker means that flights has been cancelled or seasonal and not in operation.
                 </li>
                 <li style="text-align: justify;">
                  Green marker for planned services. Time
  span mean that one or more flights will be operating during the period.
  Check the label for more information.
                 </li>
                 <li style="text-align: justify;">
                  Airplane marker means that at least one
  air carrier has service in operation all year around. More airlines may
  have seasonal flights to the destination.  Check the label for more 
 information.
                 </li>
                 <li style="text-align: justify;">
                  Activity marker means the destination 
 is predominantly a charter destination. Seasonal regular flights may 
 operate.  Check the label for more information.
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <b>
                  New flights from Bergen Airport - April 2013:
                 </b>
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   Chania - Greece (Seasonal)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Dubrovnik - Croatia (Seasonal)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Edinburgh - United Kingdom (Seasonal)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Larnaca - Cyprus (Charter)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Nice - France (Seasonal)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Palma de Mallorca - Spain (Charter / seasonal)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Warsaw - Poland (All year)
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <b>
                  Ending flights from Bergen Airport - April 2013:
                 </b>
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   Lanzarote - Spain (Charter)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Salzburg - Austria (Seasonal)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Sharm el Sheikh - Egypt (Charter)
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Tenerife - Spain (Charter)
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                </div>
               </div>

               </div>

              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/updated-bergen-z-2007-2012.html">
                UPDATED: Bergen A-Z 2007-2012
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <iframe frameborder="0" height="480" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" scrolling="no" src="http://maps.google.com/maps/ms?ie=UTF8&amp;hl=en&amp;msa=0&amp;msid=104505204180738053972.00043db82620ba51aaed6&amp;ll=60.396303,5.328712&amp;spn=0.040704,0.109863&amp;z=13&amp;output=embed" width="640">
                 </iframe>
                 <br/>
                 <small>
                  View
                  <a href="http://maps.google.com/maps/ms?ie=UTF8&amp;hl=en&amp;msa=0&amp;msid=104505204180738053972.00043db82620ba51aaed6&amp;ll=60.396303,5.328712&amp;spn=0.040704,0.109863&amp;z=13&amp;source=embed" style="color: blue; text-align: left;">
                   Bergen and Surrounding areas 2007-2012
                  </a>
                  in a larger map
                 </small>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                </span>
                <br/>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <span style="font-style: italic;">
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bergen">
                   Bergen
                  </a>
                  is the only genuine medieval city in Norway. The city centre has been ravaged by flames many times, the latest being by the large fire of 1702. Over and over has the city risen from the flames, along the same old narrow medieval streets and passages. Among the most beautiful areas is
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bryggen">
                   Bryggen
                  </a>
                  , rebuilt after the last large fire, it still reflects centuries of building tradition.
                 </span>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Here is a map and all stories written from Bergen on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel from 2006-2012 in case you would need where to go, what see, and where to eat in Norway's only medieval city. I am so pleased to  go back to this beautiful ancient city in April 2012 to attend a conference.
                </div>
                <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <br/>
                 Food stories:
                 <br/>
                </span>

                  </a>
                 </li>

                   Food Hall and Fish market
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>

                 Sights:
                </span>
                <br/>

                <div>
                 <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                  How to get to Bergen
                 </span>
                </div>
                <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                 <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_xr3cuiiS77U/SwGaTzVLSkI/AAAAAAAAKlc/56GqA1_7uRg/s1600/IMGP2379.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                  <img alt="" border="0" height="515" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5404770692808526402" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_xr3cuiiS77U/SwGaTzVLSkI/AAAAAAAAKlc/56GqA1_7uRg/s640/IMGP2379.jpg" style="float: left; height: 307px; margin: 0pt 10px 10px 0pt; width: 381px;" width="640"/>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <b>
                 <br/>
                </b>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                </span>
                <br/>
                <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
                <br/>
                <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <br/>
                </span>
                <br/>
                <span style="font-weight: bold;">
                 - By air
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 On this map you will find markers that display status on different non-stop flights from Bergen Airport to destinations in Europe. A red marker means that flights is seasonal and not in operation or that an earlier non-stop flight has been canceled. A green marker shows that there is a new non-stop flight planned to this destination. A yellow marker means that there a seasonal flight still operating to this airport. An airplane button means that service is in operation all year around from one or several European destination to Bergen.
                </div>
                <br/>
                <a href="http://maps.google.com/maps/ms?ie=UTF8&amp;source=embed&amp;msa=0&amp;msid=104505204180738053972.0004708b613b68cad72b1&amp;ll=54.977614,0.703125&amp;spn=62.261203,186.152344&amp;z=3">
                 See map of direct flights from Europe to Bergen airport Flesland
                </a>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_xr3cuiiS77U/SwGbLP0u26I/AAAAAAAAKlk/OpgB9B0t0z0/s1600/IMGP1708.jpg">
                 <img alt="" border="0" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5404771645349878690" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_xr3cuiiS77U/SwGbLP0u26I/AAAAAAAAKlk/OpgB9B0t0z0/s400/IMGP1708.jpg" style="cursor: pointer; float: left; height: 277px; margin: 0pt 10px 10px 0pt; width: 370px;"/>
                </a>

                 - By sea
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>

                 Enjoy Food &amp; Travel proudly introduce a new service to travelers from Europe to Norway. On this special map you find ferry connection from European to Norwegian ports.
                </div>
                <a href="http://maps.google.com/maps/ms?ie=UTF8&amp;hl=en&amp;source=embed&amp;msa=0&amp;msid=104505204180738053972.000470c67a0b2473b5c86&amp;ll=59.198439,6.855469&amp;spn=3.370414,11.634521&amp;z=7">

              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/easyjet-chose-bergen-as-its-norwegian.html">
                EasyJet chose Bergen as its Norwegian base
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--im-EJZ1R50/UU_zzv0-r1I/AAAAAAAAQ5o/BHTT-0uhC2A/s1600/800px-Boarding.easyjet.a319.arp.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="298" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--im-EJZ1R50/UU_zzv0-r1I/AAAAAAAAQ5o/BHTT-0uhC2A/s400/800px-Boarding.easyjet.a319.arp.jpg" width="400"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    I sincerely hope that these planes may soon be seen at Oslo Airport as well  as in Bergen . Photo: Arpingstone
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <i>
                  British budget airline
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/EasyJet" target="_blank">
                   EasyJet
                  </a>
                  has flights from most European countries, but Norway has been one of the few countries not serviced by this air carrier. This may change, as EasyJet has chosen Norway's second airport
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bergen_Flesland_Airport" target="_blank">
                   Bergen Flesland
                  </a>
                  as its base.
                 </i>
                </div>
                <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-soyfPg_lu5k/UU_2uKD8aLI/AAAAAAAAQ5w/0mgV3fS1gRg/s1600/Bergen_Airport_terminal.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="220" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-soyfPg_lu5k/UU_2uKD8aLI/AAAAAAAAQ5w/0mgV3fS1gRg/s320/Bergen_Airport_terminal.jpg" width="320"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    Bergen Flesland Airport. Photo: Arsenikk
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 EasyJet is the third biggest air carrier in Europe with more than 50 million passengers each year. It has 22 bases in Europe, and is one of Ryanair's fiercest competitors.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 The Bergen Airport management hopes that EasyJet flights to Bergen and the Norwegian West coast may boost the local travel industry.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 As a traveler, I would certainly welcome EasyJet to Norway, and hope the air carrier may challenge the growing dominance of Ryanair and Norwegian Air Shuttle.
                 <br/>
                 <b>
                  <br/>
                 </b>
                 <b>
                  Start flights Bergen - London
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 EasyJet will start its first flights from Bergen May 20th. It will challenge Norwegian Air Shuttle on flights from Bergen to London Gatwick Airport and British Airways on flights to London Heathrow. .
                </div>
               </div>
               <div style="clear: both;">
               </div>
              </div>

               </script>

          <div class="date-outer">
           <h2 class="date-header">
            <span>
             Sunday, March 24, 2013
            </span>
           </h2>
           <div class="date-posts">
            <div class="post-outer">
             <div class="post hentry">
              <a name="8401480693434857020">
              </a>
              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/confit-de-canard-du-souq-or-moroccan.html">
                Confit de Canard du Souq or Moroccan duck legs
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FXsJn6GeviQ/UU8NzQ-9ouI/AAAAAAAAQ4w/TRifa7jeYBg/s1600/220px-Piper_longum.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="300" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FXsJn6GeviQ/UU8NzQ-9ouI/AAAAAAAAQ4w/TRifa7jeYBg/s400/220px-Piper_longum.jpg" width="400"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    Piper Longum - one rare ingredient in my Moroccan duck. Photo: Lemmikkipuu
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <i>
                  Yesterday I made another
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Duck_confit" target="_blank">
                   duck confit
                  </a>
                  . This time I substituted (or added to the) salt and pepper with some very different Moroccan spices and ingredients thus the name; Confit de canard de
                  <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Souq" target="_blank">
                   Souq
                  </a>
                  , from the bazaars.
                 </i>
                </div>
                <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CaADg9cAqAY/UU8O61xMWMI/AAAAAAAAQ44/qw2f84yeqq8/s1600/743px-Ras.el.hanout.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="258" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CaADg9cAqAY/UU8O61xMWMI/AAAAAAAAQ44/qw2f84yeqq8/s320/743px-Ras.el.hanout.jpg" width="320"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    Ras el Hanout. Photo: Sarefo
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 I have described how to make a duck confit earlier, so here I will talk about the seasoning. I wanted to make duck legs with a distinct and exotic taste. What could be better than picking some of the spices I have brought back from my travels.
                </div>
                <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: left; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-puxpG8uDJG8/UU8VS9RoLWI/AAAAAAAAQ5E/2J68hWz1Rn8/s1600/735px-Spanishsmokedpaprika.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="261" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-puxpG8uDJG8/UU8VS9RoLWI/AAAAAAAAQ5E/2J68hWz1Rn8/s320/735px-Spanishsmokedpaprika.jpg" width="320"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    Red paprika powder. Photo: Bandagnani
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 For heat I took out
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Long_pepper" target="_blank">
                  piper longum or long pepper
                 </a>
                 , a very spicy variety of pepper known to Europeans as far back as ancient Greece. It is very hot, and the grains are up to 1 cm (1/2 inch) long. It is a very rare ingredient and I aqcuired it at
                 <a href="http://no.tripadvisor.com/Attraction_Review-g187147-d546504-Reviews-Izrael_Le_Monde_des_Epices-Paris_Ile_de_France.html" target="_blank">
                  Izrael, the extraordinary spice shop in Marais in Paris
                 </a>
                 .
                </div>
                <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: right; margin-left: 1em; text-align: right;">
                 <tbody>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="text-align: center;">
                    <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-v1APq8e5ZWg/UU8ZG57mNoI/AAAAAAAAQ5Q/eWOY2EKgF10/s1600/800px-DriedFigs1.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                     <img border="0" height="240" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-v1APq8e5ZWg/UU8ZG57mNoI/AAAAAAAAQ5Q/eWOY2EKgF10/s320/800px-DriedFigs1.JPG" width="320"/>
                    </a>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                    Dried figs. Photo: Rich Smith
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </tbody>
                </table>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 I pounded the pepperkorns with salt in my large morter and I sprinkled on the duck legs.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 Then I added
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ras_el_hanout" target="_blank">
                  ras el hanout
                 </a>
                 , a blend of spices from North Africa bought in the souqs of Marrakech made from
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cardamom" title="Cardamom">
                  cardamom
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Clove" title="Clove">
                  clove
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cinnamon" title="Cinnamon">
                  cinnamon
                 </a>
                 , ground
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chili_pepper" title="Chili pepper">
                  chili peppers
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Coriander" title="Coriander">
                  coriander
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cumin" title="Cumin">
                  cumin
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nutmeg" title="Nutmeg">
                  nutmeg
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a class="mw-redirect" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peppercorn_%28fruit%29" title="Peppercorn (fruit)">
                  peppercorn
                 </a>
                 , and
                 <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turmeric" title="Turmeric">
                  turmeric
                 </a>
                 .
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 The last seasoning on my Moroccan duck was also purchased in the souq, smokey red paprika powder. To add to the Moroccan theme I placed chalottes and dried figs from the bazaars in the oven proof dish. The idea was that the dried fruit would soak up the juices from the duck.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 I also drizzled a little honey over the duck legs to create balance, and allowed them to bake for 8 hours on 100 degrees Celsius (215F). By then onions and fics had taken up the aromas of the duck and the seasoning. Just like the many of the tagines served in Morocco combining savoury and sweet ingedients, I had succeeded in creating a touch of Morocco for my guests.
                </div>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <b>
                  More duck confit and duck dishes
                 </b>
                </div>
                <ul style="text-align: left;">
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2011/02/more-duck-confit-with-dried-figs.html">
                   More duck confit - with dried figs
                  </a>
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2009/05/my-stress-free-home-made-duck-confit.html">
                   Stress-free home made duck confit
                  </a>
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2009/05/delicious-crostinis-on-way-to-opera.html">
                   Delicious crostinis on the way to the opera
                  </a>
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2011/09/duck-liver-pate.html">
                   Duck liver paté
                  </a>
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/08/warm-salad-with-swiss-chard-smoked-duck.html">
                   Warm salad with Swiss chard, smoked duck breast and quail eggs
                  </a>
                 </li>
                </ul>
               </div>
               <div style="clear: both;">
               </div>
