          <div class="date-outer">
           <h2 class="date-header">
            <span>
             Saturday, March 23, 2013
            </span>
           </h2>
           <div class="date-posts">
            <div class="post-outer">
             <div class="post hentry">
              <a name="3534223298627394393">
              </a>
              <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2013/03/updated-sights-on-enjoy-food-travel-2012.html">
                UPDATED: Sights on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel 2012
               </a>
              </h3>
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
              <div class="post-body entry-content">
               <p>
               </p>
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                 <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                    <tbody style="text-align: left;">
                     <tr style="text-align: left;">
                      <td style="text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eV2HEFlC_7A/TwRuu-K22II/AAAAAAAANZo/3ggyhROQVqQ/s1600/IMGP3439.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;">
                        <img border="0" height="360" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-eV2HEFlC_7A/TwRuu-K22II/AAAAAAAANZo/3ggyhROQVqQ/s400/IMGP3439.jpg" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </td>
                     </tr>
                     <tr style="text-align: left;">
                      <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                       Mosaic at Pammakaristos Church, Istanbul Turkey
                      </td>
                     </tr>
                    </tbody>
                   </table>
                   <i>
                    To make it easier for you, I have compiled all the sights on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel for the year 2012 on this page. Enjoy!!
                   </i>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <b>
                    A
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/08/alte-brucke-heidelberg.html">
                        Alte Brucke - Heidelberg
                       </a>
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       (August 23rd 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     The old bridge or die Alte Brucke is one of the most famous sights of Heidelberg. The bridge is the ninth over the river Neckar since Roman times and dates back to 1788.
                     <br/>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </i>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/08/archbishops-palace-lima-peru.html">
                        Archbishops Palace - Lima, Peru
                       </a>
                       (August 1st 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     The current Archbishops Palace in Lima was built as late as 1924, but the Archbishops have resided here since 1530. The building is baroque in appearance.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    B
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/02/bergen-aquarium-bergen-norway.html">
                        Bergen Aquarium, Bergen Norway
                       </a>
                       (February 19th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <i>
                      <br/>
                     </i>
                     The large aquarium at the Nordnes peninsula in Bergen, Norway has, since it was opened in 1960 been one of the city's main attractions
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/07/bispegarden-troms-norway.html">
                        Bispegården - Tromsø, Norway
                       </a>
                       (July 12th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     One of the most beautiful houses in Tromsø city centre is the 
 residence of the bishop of the northern most Roman Catholic diocese in 
 the world.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/03/bosque-el-olivar-lima.html">
                        Bosque el Olivar, Lima
                       </a>
                       (March 30th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     The Bosque El Olivar is an olive grove going back 450 years, to three  trees that survived the transportation from Europe in 1560.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    C
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/07/chapel-chateau-voltaire-ferney-voltaire.html" target="_blank">
                        Chapel - Chateau Voltaire
                       </a>
                       , Ferney-Voltaire (July 2nd 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      The philosopher Voltaire erected a chapel in the park of his own Chateau in 1761. It and even the chateau itself are now in a state of disrepair, so much so that the chapel is falling down.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <span style="background-color: white;">
                      <b>
                       <i>
                        <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/18th-and-early-19th-century-buildings.html" target="_blank">
                         Crowninshield-Bentley House (ca. 1727)
                        </a>
                        , Salem MA (September 19th 2012)
                       </i>
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      This magnificent Georgian-style house was built for a captain John Crowninshield in 1727. It has been moved to its present location in 126 Essex Street.
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    D
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <i style="font-weight: bold;">
                      <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/18th-and-early-19th-century-buildings.html" target="_blank">
                       Derby House (1762)
                      </a>
                      <b>
                       Salem MA (September 19th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     The beautiful red-brick Derby House is an exquisite example of American Georgian Architecture. It   was built in 1762 as a marriage present by Elias Hasket Derby to his wife Elisabeth Crowninshield in 1762.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                       <i>
                        <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/02/destination-rros.html" target="_blank">
                         Destination Røros
                        </a>
                        (February 27th 2012)
                       </i>
                       <br/>
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-weight: normal; line-height: 16px;">
                        The old mining town Røros was founded in 1644 after a farmer discovered huge amounts of copper close by. From the mid 1600's the city grew into the most prosperous cities in the country.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </b>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    E
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <b style="font-style: italic;">
                      <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2001/12/eglise-russe-geneva.html">
                       Église Russe, Geneva, Switzerland
                      </a>
                      (January 1st 2012)
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     When strolling in Geneva City Centre we spotted these beautiful gilded domes. They belong to the Église Russe, The Russian Church.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    F
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/04/first-meeting-house-salem-ma.html">
                        First Meeting House, Salem MA
                       </a>
                       (March 14th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     Salem MA is, as one of the oldest cities in the US, filled with  historical sites commemorating the earliest stages of American history,  as this plaque telling the story about the first meeting house that  stood on this location until 1673.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <b>
                     </b>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/05/flibanen-bergen.html" target="_blank">
                        Fløibanen, Bergen
                       </a>
                       (May 6th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     Fløibanen is, in my opinion, one of the best attractions Bergen has to offer. The carts of funicular will bring you 320 meters in 7 minutes, and when up you will have a superb view over the city.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/08/fort-van-tyle-minisink-ny.html" target="_blank">
                        Fort Van Tyle
                       </a>
                       , Minisink NY (August 30th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     I love local history, and traveling around upstate New York gave me an opportunity to visit historic sights of the Port Jervis / Greenville area. We spotted this sign when driving along a quiet country road.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </div>
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   <b>
                    G
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/18th-and-early-19th-century-buildings.html" target="_blank">
                        Gardner Pingree House (1804)
                       </a>
                       ,
                      </b>
                      <b>
                       Salem MA (September 19th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     This is one of several houses in Salem designed by the famous architect Samuel McIntire. It was built in Federal style for Samuel West Gardner, but was sold on in 1814 to cover losses to Gardner caused events leading up to the War of 1812.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i style="font-weight: bold;">
                      <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/18th-and-early-19th-century-buildings.html" target="_blank">
                       Gideon Tucker House (1808)
                      </a>
                      , Salem MA (September 19th 2012)
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     The Gideon Tucker House is a third house I saw designed by Samuel McIntire. It was built for Gideon Tucker in 1808 or 1809, a man that worked as a clerk, but ended up as a wealthy businessman.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <br/>
                   <b>
                    H
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/03/hagia-irene-church-istanbul.html">
                        Hagia Irene Church, Istanbul
                       </a>
                       (March 23rd 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     Hagia Irene, located on the grounds of the Topkapi Palace,  is an ancient building. It is in fact the oldest church in Istanbul,  but most of what you see today dates from the 8th century when the  church was damaged by a eartquake.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/hamburg-rathaus.html" target="_blank">
                        Hamburg Rathaus
                       </a>
                       , Hamburg (September 8th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     Hamburg Rathaus or Hamburg City Hall is a massive building located in the heart of the city.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/18th-and-early-19th-century-buildings.html" target="_blank">
                        Hamilton Hall (1805)
                       </a>
                       , Salem MA (September 19th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     The magnificent Hamilton Hall mansion is located in 9 Chestnut Street. It was not built as a private house but as assembling hall for the Salem federalists.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/02/hauptkirche-st-jacobi-hamburg.html">
                        Hauptkirche St. Jacobi, Hamburg
                       </a>
                       (February 5th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <br/>
                     Most of what you see of Hauptkirche St. Jacobi today is rebuilt after the bombings after the war. It is dedicated to James the Great and the original structure dated back to the midt 14th century
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/17th-century-houses-of-salem-ma.html">
                        House of Seven Gables
                       </a>
                       , Salem MA (January 15th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     The oldest part of the  House of the Seven Gables  was built in 1668  for Capt. John Turner, and it remained in his family  for three generations,  descending from John Turner II to John Turner  III.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/06/huaca-pucllana-lima.html" target="_blank">
                        Huaca Pucllana
                       </a>
                       , Lima (June 5th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     Peru is famous for the Inca culture. This culture was however the latest in a long line of different cultures on which the Inca rulers built their reign. Historic monuments from these are scattered over this large country and many are also found in Lima. One of them is the Huaca Pucllana - the large pyramide.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </div>
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   <ul>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    J
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/02/jet-deau-geneva-signature.html" target="_blank">
                        Jet d'Eau - a Geneva signature
                       </a>
                       (February 26th 2012)
                      </i>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-weight: normal; line-height: 16px;">
                        The Jet d'Eau or the water jet is an impressive fountain is the signature of the city of Geneva, Switzerland
                       </span>
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-weight: normal; line-height: 16px;">
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                     </b>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-weight: bold;">
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/09/18th-and-early-19th-century-buildings.html" target="_blank">
                        Jonathan Archer House
                       </a>
                       , Salem, MA (September 19th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     The gray wooden building in 8 Hawthorne Boulevard is over 300 years old and was built by cordwainer Jonathan Archer in 1710.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/17th-century-houses-of-salem-ma.html">
                        Jonathan Corwin House
                       </a>
                       , Salem, MA (January 15th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     The home of Judge Jonathan Corwin is built around 1660 and is a beautiful example of 17th century architecture.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <b>
                    K
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/04/koutoubia-mosque-marrakech.html" target="_blank">
                        Koutoubia Mosque - Marrakech
                       </a>
                       (April 25th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     If there is a trademark of Marrakech it has to be the Koutoubia Mosque. It is by far the oldest and largest mosque in the city dating back over 800 years.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <br/>
                   <b>
                    L
                   </b>
                  </div>
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/17th-century-houses-of-salem-ma.html">
                        London Coffee House
                       </a>
                       , Salem MA (January 15th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     This late 17th century building was the gathering place of the Patriots before  the American Revolution.
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </div>
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   <b>
                    M
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   <ul>
                    <li>
                     <i>
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/03/medieval-copenhagen.html" target="_blank">
                        Medieval Copenhagen
                       </a>
                       (March 4th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     Copehagen City museum is located in Fredriksberg in central  Copenhagen. Outside the museum you find a model of how Copenhagen looked  like in the middle ages.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <i>
                      <br/>
                     </i>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <b>
                      <i>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/11/the-old-and-new-minot-light.html" target="_blank">
                        Minot light
                       </a>
                       , Cohasset, MA (November 20th 2012)
                      </i>
                     </b>
                     <br/>
                     The present Minot Lighthouse is located on a granite rock off the coast of Cohasset and Scituate MA. When looking out she grows out of the sea and it is barely visible to the naked eye. The first tower was erected 1850 and disappeared ten years later in dramatic events.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/02/miss-fan-ghost-of-dimmick-inn.html" target="_blank">
                        Miss Fan - the ghost of Dimmick Inn
                       </a>
                       (February 23rd 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: inherit; line-height: 16px; text-align: left;">
                      Dimmick Inn is daid to have a ghost that haunts them. Ms. Fan or Miss Frances Dimmick is said to roam around the old building.
                     </span>
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/marrakech-mosque-of-golden-apples.html">
                        Mosque of the Golden Apples (Mosque El Mansour)
                       </a>
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <i style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       Marrakech (January 29th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <span style="text-align: left;">
                      The Mosque El Mansour or Mosque of the Golden Apples is one out of  three main mosques in Marrakech and the largest mosque in the Kasbah  area.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </span>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     <i style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/02/more-treasures-of-musee-des-beaux-arts.html">
                        Musée des beaux-arts de Lyon
                       </a>
                       , Lyon (February 14th 2012)
                      </b>
                     </i>
                     <span style="text-align: left;">
                      Musée  des beaux-arts de Lyon has a beautiful collection of art spanning  thousands of years. Here are a few of them from very different periods  of human history.
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <b>
                 O
                </b>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <ul>
                 <li>
                  <b>
                   <i>
                    <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/05/oriental-treasures-of-peabody-essex.html" target="_blank">
                     Oriental treasures of the Peabody Essex Museum (May 21st 2012)
                    </a>
                   </i>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  The Peabody Essex Museum in Salem MA has an extra collection of artifacts, many of them from the Far East. Here are a few that I saw during my visit in October 2010.
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <br/>
                <b>
                 P
                </b>
                <br/>
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/palm-house-gothenburg.html">
                      Palmhuset
                     </a>
                     , Gothenburg Sweden (January 22nd 2012)
                     <br/>
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   I love botanical gardens and in particular green houses with tropical  flowers. In Gothenburg city centre you find a horticultural gem, a  large green house filled with most exquisite tropical plants and trees.
                   <br/>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </b>
                   </i>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/pammakaristos-church-istanbul.html">
                      Pammakaristos Church, Istanbul, Turkey
                     </a>
                     (January 8th 2012)
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   <br style="font-family: inherit;"/>
                   <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                    Pammakaristos Church in Istanbul is one of the most beautiful  churches I have ever seen. Hidden behind the rather gray facade is an  850 year old art treasure.
                   </span>
                   <br/>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <br/>
                    </b>
                   </i>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/07/paris-medieval-houses-in-rue-francois.html">
                      Paris: Medieval houses in Rue François Miron
                     </a>
                     (July 26th 2012)
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   <br/>
                   When walking down Rue François Miron, I found that this was not true.
  One of the houses in this street predates the alchymists house by at 
 least 70 years.
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/06/philosophen-weg-or-philosophers-walk.html">
                      Philosophen weg or the philosophers' walk - Heidelberg
                     </a>
                     (D) (June 12th 2012)
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   <br/>
                   A great way to start your sightseeing in Heidelberg is to take the scenic Philosophers' Walk where you can enjoy a great view of the valley and the old town.
                   <br/>
                   <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                    <br/>
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/17th-century-houses-of-salem-ma.html">
                      Pickering House
                     </a>
                     , Salem MA (January 15th 2012)
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   <br/>
                   The Pickering House  is the oldest house in Salem, dating back 350 years. It is also the  home of 10 generations of the Pickering family, making it the oldest  house in the United States continuously occupied by one family.
                   <br/>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                    </b>
                   </i>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/01/17th-century-houses-of-salem-ma.html">
                      Pickman House
                     </a>
                     , Salem MA (January 15th 2012)
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   <br/>
                   The Pickman House is located by the Old Burying Ground, the second oldest cemetery in the United States.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <i>
                    <b>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/06/place-de-vosges-jewel-of-marais.html">
                      Place de Vosges - a jewel of the Marais district
                     </a>
                     , Paris (F) (June 15th 2012)
                    </b>
                   </i>
                   <br/>
                   The Marais district of Paris is one of the areas of the French capital that escaped the urban planners of the 19th century.
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <b>
                  Q
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <b>
                    <i>
                     <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/08/qubba-fatima-zohra-marrakech.html">
                      Qubba Fatima Zohra - Marrakech
                     </a>
                     (August 8th 2012)
                    </i>
                   </b>
                   <br/>
                   By the Koutobia Mosque you will see a small, white building. It is the 400 year old Qubba or mausoleum of the famous Fatima Zohra.
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                 <b>
                  S
                 </b>
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                 </ul>
                </div>
                <ul style="text-align: left;">
                 <li>
                  <i>
                   <b>
                    <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/06/st-pers-church-ruin-sigtuna-sweden.html">
                     St. Pers Church Ruin - Sigtuna, Sweden
                    </a>
                    (June 25th 2012)
                   </b>
                  </i>
                  <br/>
                  Church of Sankt Per’s (or St. Peter’s) used to be the main church of the Archdiocese before it was moved to the city of Uppsala.
                  <br/>
                  <b>
                   <i>
                    <br/>
                   </i>
                  </b>
                 </li>
                 <li>
                  <b>
                   <i>
                    <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/06/speicherstadt-hamburg.html">
                     Speicherstadt - Hamburg (D)
                    </a>
                    (June 18th 2012)
                   </i>
                  </b>
                  <br/>
                  <div style="text-align: justify;">
                   Speicherstadt is Hamburgs warehouse district. It has, during the last
  years, gone through an extensive restoration the last decade, and is 
 today one of the most beautiful areas of Hamburg.
                  </div>
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <b>
                 T
                </b>
                <br/>
                <ul style="text-align: left;">
                 <li>
                  <h3 class="post-title entry-title" style="color: #333333; line-height: 1.1em; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                   <span style="color: #333333; font-family: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
                    <i>
                     <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: small;">
                      <a href="http://www.enjoyfoodtravel.com/2012/07/tomb-of-suleyman-great-istanbul.html" target="_blank">
                       Tomb of Suleyman the Great, Istanbul
                      </a>
                      (July 12th 2012)
                     </span>
                    </i>
                   </span>
                   <div style="text-align: left;">
                    <span style="color: #333333; font-family: inherit; text-decoration: none;">
                     <span style="font-weight: normal; line-height: 16px; text-align: justify;">
                      <span style="font-family: inherit; font-size: small;">
                       Suleyman I (Ottoman Turkish: سليمان Sulaymān, Turkish: Süleyman) died on September 6th 1566) after 46 years on the throne. He was known in the West as "the Magnificent" but is most often referred to as "the Lawgiver."
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </div>
                  </h3>
                 </li>
                </ul>
                <iframe frameborder="0" height="480" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" scrolling="no" src="http://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.0004b5b165292128d02bd&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;vpsrc=6&amp;ll=29.22889,22.5&amp;spn=121.962479,225&amp;z=2&amp;output=embed" width="640">
                </iframe>
                <br/>
                <small>
                 View
                 <a href="http://maps.google.com/maps/ms?msa=0&amp;msid=211515860152448114978.0004b5b165292128d02bd&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;t=m&amp;vpsrc=6&amp;ll=29.22889,22.5&amp;spn=121.962479,225&amp;z=2&amp;source=embed" style="color: blue; text-align: left;">
                  Sights on Enjoy Food &amp; Travel 2012
                 </a>
                 in a larger map
                </small>
               </div>
               <div style="clear: both;">
               </div>
              </div>
